THE UK NOTAM OFFICE WILL IMPLEMENT THE FOLLOWING CHANGES TO THEIR
NOTAM SERIES WEF 02 OCT.
THE FOLLOWING AD WILL BE DISTRIBUTED IN THE INDIA SERIES: ABERDEEN,
ALDERGROVE, BELFAST CITY, EDINBURGH, GLASGOW, INVERNESS, NEWCASTLE,
PRESTWICK AND SUMBURGH.
COMBINING THE K AND N SERIES - THE K SERIES WILL BE REMOVED AND BE 
COVERED BY THE N SERIES.
COMBINING THE D AND F SERIES - THE F SERIES NOTAM WILL BE REMOVED 
AND COVERED BY THE D SERIES.
COMBINING THE Q AND U SERIES - THE Q SERIES NOTAM WILL BE REMOVED 
AND COVERED BY THE U SERIES.
CHANGE OF SERIES FOR NOTAM THAT HAVE AN AD IN FIELD A - ALL NAV 
WARNINGS WITH AN AD IN FIELD A WILL BE ISSUED UNDER THAT AD SERIES.
ALL NAV AIDS WITH AN AD IN FIELD A WILL BE ISSUED UNDER THAT AD 
SERIES.
AIRSPACE NOTAM WITH AN AD IN FIELD A WILL BE ISSUED UNDER THAT AD 
SERIES. WITH THE EXCEPTION OF UNLICENSED AD (E SERIES) AND THOSE 
CATERED FOR IN THE J SERIES.
NOTAM WITH A START DATE AFTER 02 OCT WILL BE ISSUED IN THEIR NEW 
SERIES.
AFTN ADDRESSES WILL BE AMENDED TO REFLECT THE CHANGES. USERS ARE 
REMINDED THAT IT IS THEIR RESPONSIBILITY TO ENSURE THEY REVIEW ALL 
NOTAM SERIES RELEVANT TO THEIR REQUIREMENTS. SHOULD ANY USER WISH
TO BE 'ADDED TO' OR 'REMOVED FROM' DISTRIBUTION LISTS, THEY SHOULD 
EMAIL THEIR REQUEST TO NOTAM.PROPOSALS(AT)NATS.CO.UK ADVISING OF
THE AFTN ADDRESS AND NOTAM SERIES THE CHANGE AFFECTS. FURTHER 
DETAILS ARE CONTAINED IN AIC Y142/25. THIS NOTAM SUPERSEDES UK AIP 
GEN 3.1, PARAGRAPH 3.6.3.4 TABLE - UK NOTAM SERIES.
